```
import os
import requests
import json
from datetime import datetime

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print("API key found, proceeding with targeted verification search...")
print("=" * 80)
print("VERIFYING 2011 ELSEVIER PUBLICATION: 'Extractive Metallurgy of Nickel, Cobalt and Platinum-Group Metals'")
print("=" * 80)

# Define highly specific search queries to verify the publication contains both required processes
verification_queries = [
'"Extractive Metallurgy of Nickel, Cobalt and Platinum-Group Metals" 2011 Elsevier calcination lithium salts automotive catalysts',
'"Extractive Metallurgy of Nickel, Cobalt and Platinum-Group Metals" 2011 bioleaching Acidithiobacillus thiooxidans cobalt',
'"Extractive Metallurgy of Nickel, Cobalt and Platinum-Group Metals" table of contents chapters',
'"Extractive Metallurgy of Nickel, Cobalt and Platinum-Group Metals" 2011 Elsevier review summary',
'Elsevier 2011 "calcination process lithium salts" "spent automotive catalysts" nickel cobalt platinum',
'Elsevier 2011 "two-stage bioleaching" "Acidithiobacillus thiooxidans" "low-grade cobalt ores"',
'"Extractive Metallurgy of Nickel, Cobalt and Platinum-Group Metals" publisher catalog description',
'ScienceDirect "Extractive Metallurgy of Nickel, Cobalt and Platinum-Group Metals" 2011 chapters'
]

print(f"Executing {len(verification_queries)} targeted verification searches...\n")

# Store all verification results
verification_results = []

for i, query in enumerate(verification_queries, 1):
print(f"Verification Search {i}/{len(verification_queries)}: {query}")
print("-" * 60)

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 15, # Increased number for better coverage
"type": "search"
}

try:
# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()

if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results")

# Store results with query context
query_results = {
'query': query,
'results': results['organic_results'],
'search_number': i,
'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
}
verification_results.append(query_results)

# Display and analyze top results for this query
relevant_found = False
for j, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'][:8], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No URL')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

# Check for highly relevant indicators
title_lower = title.lower()
snippet_lower = snippet.lower()
combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}"

# Key indicators for the specific publication
key_indicators = [
'extractive metallurgy of nickel, cobalt and platinum-group metals',
'calcination process',
'lithium salts',
'automotive catalysts',
'bioleaching',
'acidithiobacillus thiooxidans',
'cobalt ores',
'elsevier',
'2011'
]

matching_indicators = [ind for ind in key_indicators if ind in combined_text]

print(f"\n Result {j}:")
print(f" Title: {title}")
print(f" URL: {link}")
print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:300]}{'...' if len(snippet) > 300 else ''}")

if matching_indicators:
print(f" ‚≠ê MATCHING INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}")
relevant_found = True

# Special attention to publisher sites, academic databases, and book catalogs
if any(domain in link.lower() for domain in ['elsevier', 'sciencedirect', 'springer', 'wiley', 'worldcat', 'amazon', 'google.com/books']):
print(f" üéØ HIGH-PRIORITY SOURCE: Publisher/Academic database result")

if not relevant_found:
print(" No highly relevant results found for this query")

else:
print("No organic results found for this query")
verification_results.append({
'query': query,
'results': [],
'search_number': i,
'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
})
else:
print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error during verification search {i}: {str(e)}")
continue

print("\n")

print("\n" + "=" * 80)
print("VERIFICATION ANALYSIS SUMMARY")
print("=" * 80)

# Save all verification results to workspace for detailed analysis
timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
results_file = f"workspace/elsevier_2011_verification_results_{timestamp}.json"

with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump({
'publication_title': 'Extractive Metallurgy of Nickel, Cobalt and Platinum-Group Metals',
'publication_year': '2011',
'publisher': 'Elsevier',
'verification_timestamp': timestamp,
'total_queries': len(verification_queries),
'queries_executed': verification_queries,
'verification_results': verification_results
}, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"Verification results saved to: {results_file}")

# Analyze findings
total_results = sum(len(query_result['results']) for query_result in verification_results)
print(f"Total verification results collected: {total_results}")

# Look for direct publication matches
direct_matches = []
calcination_mentions = []
bioleaching_mentions = []
elsevier_2011_matches = []

for query_result in verification_results:
for result in query_result['results']:
title = result.get('title', '').lower()
snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower()
link = result.get('link', '').lower()
combined = f"{title} {snippet} {link}"

# Direct publication title matches
if 'extractive metallurgy of nickel, cobalt and platinum-group metals' in combined:
direct_matches.append({
'query': query_result['query'],
'title': result.get('title'),
'link': result.get('link'),
'snippet': result.get('snippet')
})

# Calcination process mentions
if 'calcination' in combined and ('lithium' in combined or 'automotive' in combined or 'catalyst' in combined):
calcination_mentions.append({
'query': query_result['query'],
'title': result.get('title'),
'link': result.get('link'),
'snippet': result.get('snippet')
})

# Bioleaching mentions
if 'bioleaching' in combined and ('acidithiobacillus' in combined or 'thiooxidans' in combined or 'cobalt' in combined):
bioleaching_mentions.append({
'query': query_result['query'],
'title': result.get('title'),
'link': result.get('link'),
'snippet': result.get('snippet')
})

# Elsevier 2011 matches
if 'elsevier' in combined and '2011' in combined:
elsevier_2011_matches.append({
'query': query_result['query'],
'title': result.get('title'),
'link': result.get('link'),
'snippet': result.get('snippet')
})

print(f"\nüìä VERIFICATION FINDINGS:")
print(f"Direct publication title matches: {len(direct_matches)}")
print(f"Calcination process mentions: {len(calcination_mentions)}")
print(f"Bioleaching process mentions: {len(bioleaching_mentions)}")
print(f"Elsevier 2011 matches: {len(elsevier_2011_matches)}")

if direct_matches:
print(f"\nüéØ DIRECT PUBLICATION MATCHES FOUND:")
for i, match in enumerate(direct_matches[:5], 1):
print(f" {i}. {match['title']}")
print(f" URL: {match['link']}")
print(f" Query: {match['query']}")
print(f" Snippet: {match['snippet'][:200]}...")
print()

if calcination_mentions:
print(f"\n‚öóÔ∏è CALCINATION PROCESS MENTIONS:")
for i, mention in enumerate(calcination_mentions[:3], 1):
print(f" {i}. {mention['title']}")
print(f" Snippet: {mention['snippet'][:150]}...")
print()

if bioleaching_mentions:
print(f"\nü¶† BIOLEACHING PROCESS MENTIONS:")
for i, mention in enumerate(bioleaching_mentions[:3], 1):
print(f" {i}. {mention['title']}")
print(f" Snippet: {mention['snippet'][:150]}...")
print()

print(f"\nüìã VERIFICATION STATUS:")
if direct_matches and (calcination_mentions or bioleaching_mentions):
print("‚úÖ PUBLICATION IDENTIFIED with some process mentions")
print(" - Direct publication matches found")
print(" - Some relevant process mentions detected")
print(" - Requires deeper analysis of specific chapters/content")
elif direct_matches:
print("‚ö†Ô∏è PUBLICATION IDENTIFIED but limited process verification")
print(" - Direct publication matches found")
print(" - Limited specific process mentions")
print(" - May require access to full publication content")
else:
print("‚ùå LIMITED VERIFICATION RESULTS")
print(" - No direct publication title matches")
print(" - May need alternative search strategies")
print(" - Publication may not be widely indexed or accessible")

print(f"\nDetailed verification data saved to: {results_file}")
print("Ready for next phase: detailed content analysis if publication is confirmed.")
```

### Development Step 7: Access 2020 Nature.com Chinstrap Penguin Global Population Study; Extract Figures and Methodology

**Description**: Search for and access the Nature.com article titled 'global population assessment of the Chinstrap penguin' from 2020. Extract the specific population figure from this study, noting whether it's provided as breeding pairs or individual penguins. Document the exact methodology and population count to enable accurate comparison with the Wikipedia 2018 data.

**Use Cases**:
- Wildlife conservation policy development and regulatory compliance tracking for environmental agencies extracting Chinstrap penguin counts and survey methods to inform protected area management
- Automated meta-analysis pipeline for ecological research labs harvesting 2020 population figures and methodologies for comparative species trend studies
- Environmental NGO report generation and stakeholder presentations incorporating precise breeding-pair data from Nature studies into annual conservation impact reports
- Marine biology curriculum content creation using extracted global population figures and field census techniques as real-world case studies for university courses
- Integration of structured penguin population data into open biodiversity platforms and JSON databases to support public research and citizen science initiatives
- Climate change impact modeling workflow for research institutes feeding standardized population metrics into ecosystem simulation models to forecast Antarctic biodiversity shifts
- Journalistic fact-checking and science news enrichment verifying reported Chinstrap penguin numbers and methodology details when covering Nature.com publications
- Automated updates to Wikipedia species entries comparing 2020 Nature study data with 2018 figures and generating structured update recommendations for editors

```
import os
import re
import json

print("=== PARSING 2020 NATURE STUDY FOR POPULATION FIGURES ===\n")

# Locate workspace directory
workspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir('.') if d.startswith('workspace')]
if not workspace_dirs:
print("No workspace directory found.")
exit()

workspace_dir = workspace_dirs[0]
print(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\n")

# Load the correct 2020 study text file
study_text_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'nature_chinstrap_2020_study_text.txt')
if not os.path.exists(study_text_file):
print(f"Study text file not found: {study_text_file}")
exit()

print(f"Reading study text file: {os.path.basename(study_text_file)}")
with open(study_text_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
study_text = f.read()

print(f"Study text length: {len(study_text):,} characters\n")

# First, let's examine the overall structure and find key sections
print("=== IDENTIFYING KEY SECTIONS IN THE STUDY ===\n")

# Look for major section headings
section_patterns = [
r'Abstract',
r'Introduction',
r'Results',
r'Discussion',
r'Methods',
r'Conclusion'
]

found_sections = []
for pattern in section_patterns:
matches = list(re.finditer(pattern, study_text, re.IGNORECASE))
if matches:
for match in matches:
found_sections.append({
'section': pattern,
'position': match.start(),
'text': match.group()
})

# Sort sections by position
found_sections.sort(key=lambda x: x['position'])

print("Major sections found:")
for section in found_sections:
print(f" - {section['section']} at position {section['position']:,}")

# Extract key population-related numbers and methodology
print("\n=== SEARCHING FOR POPULATION FIGURES ===\n")

# Patterns to look for population numbers
population_patterns = [
r'(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:breeding\s*pairs?|pairs?)',
r'(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:individuals?|penguins?)',
r'population\s+of\s+(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)',
r'total\s+(?:of\s+)?(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:breeding\s*pairs?|pairs?|individuals?)',
r'estimated\s+(?:at\s+)?(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:breeding\s*pairs?|pairs?|individuals?)',
r'global\s+population\s+(?:of\s+)?(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)',
r'approximately\s+(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:breeding\s*pairs?|pairs?|individuals?)'
]

population_findings = []

for pattern in population_patterns:
matches = list(re.finditer(pattern, study_text, re.IGNORECASE))
for match in matches:
# Get context around the match (200 characters before and after)
start = max(0, match.start() - 200)
end = min(len(study_text), match.end() + 200)
context = study_text[start:end]

population_findings.append({
'pattern': pattern,
'match': match.group(),
'number': match.group(1) if match.groups() else 'N/A',
'position': match.start(),
'context': context.replace('\n', ' ').strip()
})

print(f"Found {len(population_findings)} potential population references:")
for i, finding in enumerate(population_findings, 1):
print(f"\nFinding {i}:")
print(f" Match: {finding['match']}")
print(f" Number: {finding['number']}")
print(f" Position: {finding['position']:,}")
print(f" Context: ...{finding['context'][:300]}...")

# Look specifically for key result statements
print("\n=== SEARCHING FOR KEY RESULT STATEMENTS ===\n")

# Look for sentences containing key result phrases
result_patterns = [
r'[^.]*global\s+population[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*breeding\s+pairs?[^.]*\d[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*total[^.]*population[^.]*\d[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*census[^.]*\d[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*estimate[^.]*\d[^.]*breeding[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*\d[^.]*million[^.]*pairs?[^.]*\.'
]

key_statements = []
for pattern in result_patterns:
matches = list(re.finditer(pattern, study_text, re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL))
for match in matches:
statement = match.group().strip()
# Clean up the statement
statement = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', statement)

key_statements.append({
'pattern': pattern,
'statement': statement,
'position': match.start()
})

print(f"Found {len(key_statements)} key result statements:")
for i, stmt in enumerate(key_statements, 1):
print(f"\nStatement {i}:")
print(f" Position: {stmt['position']:,}")
print(f" Text: {stmt['statement']}")

# Look for methodology section
print("\n=== EXTRACTING METHODOLOGY INFORMATION ===\n")

# Find methods section
methods_match = re.search(r'Methods?\s*\n?([\s\S]*?)(?=\n\s*(?:Results?|Discussion|Conclusion|References?|Acknowledgments?)\s*\n|$)', study_text, re.IGNORECASE)

if methods_match:
methods_text = methods_match.group(1)[:2000] # First 2000 characters
print("Methods section found (first 2000 characters):")
print(methods_text)

# Look for specific methodology terms
method_terms = ['survey', 'census', 'count', 'observation', 'field', 'colony', 'site']
found_method_terms = [term for term in method_terms if term.lower() in methods_text.lower()]
print(f"\nMethodology terms found: {found_method_terms}")
else:
print("Methods section not clearly identified")

# Look for abstract for concise population summary
print("\n=== EXTRACTING ABSTRACT FOR POPULATION SUMMARY ===\n")

abstract_match = re.search(r'Abstract\s*\n?([\s\S]*?)(?=\n\s*(?:Introduction|Keywords?)\s*\n|$)', study_text, re.IGNORECASE)

if abstract_match:
abstract_text = abstract_match.group(1)[:1500] # First 1500 characters
print("Abstract found (first 1500 characters):")
print(abstract_text)

# Extract numbers from abstract
abstract_numbers = re.findall(r'\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?', abstract_text)
print(f"\nNumbers found in abstract: {abstract_numbers}")
else:
print("Abstract section not clearly identified")

# Save comprehensive analysis
analysis_results = {
'study_info': {
'title': 'A global population assessment of the Chinstrap penguin (Pygoscelis antarctica)',
'year': 2020,
'source': 'Nature.com Scientific Reports',
'text_length': len(study_text)
},
'sections_found': found_sections,
'population_findings': population_findings,
'key_statements': key_statements,
'methods_text': methods_text if 'methods_text' in locals() else 'Not extracted',
'abstract_text': abstract_text if 'abstract_text' in locals() else 'Not extracted',
'abstract_numbers': abstract_numbers if 'abstract_numbers' in locals() else []
}

analysis_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'nature_2020_population_analysis.json')
with open(analysis_file, 'w') as f:
json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2, default=str)

print(f"\n=== ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\n")
print(f"Comprehensive analysis saved to: {analysis_file}")
print(f"Population findings: {len(population_findings)}")
print(f"Key statements: {len(key_statements)}")
print(f"Sections identified: {len(found_sections)}")

print("\nNext step: Review findings to identify the specific global population figure and methodology")
```

### Development Step 5: Access 2020 Nature.com Chinstrap Penguin Population Study: Extract Count & Methodology for 2018 Comparison

**Description**: Search for and access the Nature.com article titled 'global population assessment of the Chinstrap penguin' from 2020. Extract the specific population figure from this study, noting whether it's provided as breeding pairs or individual penguins. Document the exact methodology and population count to enable accurate comparison with the Wikipedia 2018 data.

**Use Cases**:
- Wildlife conservation NGOs sourcing the latest Chinstrap penguin population figures and methodologies to prioritize colony protection efforts in Antarctica
- University ecology researchers comparing 2020 Nature.com breeding pair estimates with 2018 Wikipedia counts for peer-reviewed longitudinal studies on penguin demographics
- Environmental consultants integrating authoritative Chinstrap penguin numbers into Antarctic tourism impact assessments for compliance with sustainability regulations
- Automated monitoring pipelines extracting updated population data and sampling methods to trigger alerts when Chinstrap penguin counts deviate beyond threshold in ecological dashboards
- Data journalism teams retrieving precise penguin population metrics and survey techniques to create interactive articles on wildlife conservation trends
- Government wildlife agencies extracting standardized population figures from peer-reviewed studies to inform national biodiversity action plans and policy decisions
- E-learning content developers incorporating verified Chinstrap penguin population data and research methods into interactive modules on polar ecosystems
- Citizen science platforms validating volunteer-submitted colony count data against professional population assessments for accuracy and training feedback

```
import os
import re
import requests
import json
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

print("=== SEARCHING FOR NATURE.COM CHINSTRAP PENGUIN POPULATION STUDY (2020) ===\n")

# Search for the specific Nature.com article about Chinstrap penguin global population assessment from 2020
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print("API key found. Proceeding with search...\n")

# Construct specific search query for Nature.com Chinstrap penguin study
query = 'site:nature.com "global population assessment" "Chinstrap penguin" 2020'

print(f"Search query: {query}")

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 10,
"type": "search"
}

# Make API request to SerpAPI
print("\nMaking search request...")
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
print(f"Search completed successfully. Status code: {response.status_code}")

# Check if we have organic results
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"\nFound {len(results['organic_results'])} search results:\n")

nature_articles = []

for i, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"Result {i}:")
print(f" Title: {title}")
print(f" URL: {link}")
print(f" Snippet: {snippet}")
print()

# Check if this is a Nature.com article about Chinstrap penguins
if ('nature.com' in link.lower() and
('chinstrap' in title.lower() or 'chinstrap' in snippet.lower()) and
('population' in title.lower() or 'population' in snippet.lower()) and
'2020' in (title + snippet)):

nature_articles.append({
'title': title,
'url': link,
'snippet': snippet,
'result_number': i
})
print(f" *** IDENTIFIED AS TARGET NATURE ARTICLE ***")

# Save search results for reference
search_results_data = {
'search_query': query,
'total_results': len(results['organic_results']),
'nature_articles_found': len(nature_articles),
'all_results': results['organic_results'],
'identified_nature_articles': nature_articles
}

with open('workspace/nature_chinstrap_search_results.json', 'w') as f:
json.dump(search_results_data, f, indent=2)

print(f"\n=== SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY ===")
print(f"Total search results: {len(results['organic_results'])}")
print(f"Nature.com articles identified: {len(nature_articles)}")

if nature_articles:
print("\n=== IDENTIFIED NATURE.COM ARTICLES ===")
for article in nature_articles:
print(f"\nArticle {article['result_number']}:")
print(f"Title: {article['title']}")
print(f"URL: {article['url']}")
print(f"Snippet: {article['snippet']}")

# Try to access the first Nature article found
target_article = nature_articles[0]
print(f"\n=== ATTEMPTING TO ACCESS TARGET ARTICLE ===")
print(f"Target URL: {target_article['url']}")

# Set up headers to mimic browser request
headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36',
'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8',
'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5',
'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate',
'Connection': 'keep-alive'
}

try:
article_response = requests.get(target_article['url'], headers=headers, timeout=30)

if article_response.status_code == 200:
print(f"Successfully accessed article. Status code: {article_response.status_code}")
print(f"Content length: {len(article_response.content):,} bytes")

# Save the article HTML for analysis
with open('workspace/nature_chinstrap_article.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(article_response.text)

print(f"\nArticle HTML saved to: workspace/nature_chinstrap_article.html")

# Parse the article content
soup = BeautifulSoup(article_response.text, 'html.parser')

# Extract key information
article_title = soup.find('title')
if article_title:
print(f"\nArticle title: {article_title.get_text().strip()}")

# Look for article content containers
content_selectors = [
'div[data-test="article-content"]',
'div.c-article-body',
'article',
'div.article-item-body',
'main'
]

article_content = None
for selector in content_selectors:
content_element = soup.select_one(selector)
if content_element:
article_content = content_element
print(f"Found article content using selector: {selector}")
break

if article_content:
content_text = article_content.get_text()
print(f"\nExtracted content length: {len(content_text):,} characters")

# Save extracted text for further analysis
with open('workspace/nature_chinstrap_article_text.txt', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(content_text)

print(f"Article text saved to: workspace/nature_chinstrap_article_text.txt")
else:
print("Could not locate article content with standard selectors")
print("Will need to analyze full HTML structure")

else:
print(f"Failed to access article. Status code: {article_response.status_code}")
print(f"Response: {article_response.text[:500]}...")

except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
print(f"Error accessing article: {e}")
else:
print("\nNo Nature.com articles found for Chinstrap penguin population assessment.")
print("Will try broader search terms...")

else:
print("No search results found. Trying alternative search...")

else:
print(f"Search request failed. Status code: {response.status_code}")
print(f"Error response: {response.text}")

print(f"\n=== SEARCH PHASE COMPLETE ===")
print("Files created in workspace/:")
print(" - nature_chinstrap_search_results.json (search results data)")
if os.path.exists('workspace/nature_chinstrap_article.html'):
print(" - nature_chinstrap_article.html (full article HTML)")
if os.path.exists('workspace/nature_chinstrap_article_text.txt'):
print(" - nature_chinstrap_article_text.txt (extracted article text)")

print("\nNext step: Parse the downloaded article to extract population figures and methodology")

import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime print("=== SEARCHING FOR 2023 IPCC REPORT WITH 85-PAGE SPECIFICATION ===") print("=" * 70) # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with targeted search for 2023 IPCC 85-page report...") print() # Define specific search queries to locate the 2023 IPCC report with 85 pages search_queries = [ 'IPCC 2023 report 85 pages filetype:pdf', 'IPCC 2023 "85 pages" summary policymakers filetype:pdf', 'IPCC 2023 synthesis report 85 pages filetype:pdf', 'site:ipcc.ch 2023 report "85 pages" filetype:pdf', 'IPCC AR6 2023 synthesis report 85 pages', '"IPCC 2023" "85-page" OR "85 page" report filetype:pdf', 'IPCC sixth assessment 2023 synthesis 85 pages', 'IPCC AR6 synthesis report 2023 policymakers 85' ] print(f"Executing {len(search_queries)} targeted searches for 2023 IPCC 85-page report...\n") # Store all search results all_search_results = [] potential_reports = [] for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"Search {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 50) # Prepare API request parameters params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 15, "type": "search" } try: # Make API request to SerpAPI response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Store results with query context query_results = { 'query': query, 'results': results['organic_results'], 'search_number': i, 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() } all_search_results.append(query_results) # Analyze results for IPCC reports for j, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No URL') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') # Check for IPCC-specific indicators title_lower = title.lower() snippet_lower = snippet.lower() combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}" # Key indicators for IPCC 2023 reports ipcc_indicators = [ 'ipcc', '2023', 'synthesis', 'summary', 'policymakers', 'assessment', 'climate change', 'ar6' ] # Page count indicators page_indicators = ['85', 'page', 'pages'] matching_ipcc = [ind for ind in ipcc_indicators if ind in combined_text] matching_pages = [ind for ind in page_indicators if ind in combined_text] print(f"\n Result {j}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:200]}{'...' if len(snippet) > 200 else ''}") if matching_ipcc: print(f" ‚úì IPCC INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_ipcc)}") if matching_pages: print(f" üìÑ PAGE INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_pages)}") # High priority for official IPCC sites and PDF files is_official_ipcc = 'ipcc.ch' in link.lower() is_pdf = link.lower().endswith('.pdf') or 'filetype:pdf' in query has_2023 = '2023' in combined_text has_85_pages = '85' in combined_text and ('page' in combined_text) if is_official_ipcc: print(f" üèõÔ∏è OFFICIAL IPCC SOURCE") if is_pdf: print(f" üìã PDF DOCUMENT") if has_85_pages: print(f" üéØ 85-PAGE SPECIFICATION MENTIONED") # Score potential matches score = 0 if is_official_ipcc: score += 5 if is_pdf: score += 3 if has_2023: score += 3 if has_85_pages: score += 4 if 'synthesis' in combined_text: score += 2 if 'summary' in combined_text: score += 2 if 'policymakers' in combined_text: score += 2 if score >= 8: # High-confidence matches potential_reports.append({ 'title': title, 'url': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'query': query, 'score': score, 'indicators': { 'official_ipcc': is_official_ipcc, 'is_pdf': is_pdf, 'has_2023': has_2023, 'has_85_pages': has_85_pages, 'matching_ipcc_terms': matching_ipcc, 'matching_page_terms': matching_pages } }) print(f" ‚≠ê HIGH-CONFIDENCE MATCH (Score: {score})") else: print("No organic results found for this query") all_search_results.append({ 'query': query, 'results': [], 'search_number': i, 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() }) else: print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error during search {i}: {str(e)}") continue print("\n") print("\n" + "=" * 70) print("SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY") print("=" * 70) # Save all search results to workspace timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") results_file = f"workspace/ipcc_2023_85page_search_results_{timestamp}.json" with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump({ 'search_timestamp': timestamp, 'total_queries': len(search_queries), 'queries_executed': search_queries, 'all_search_results': all_search_results, 'potential_reports': potential_reports }, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"Search results saved to: {results_file}") # Analyze findings total_results = sum(len(query_result['results']) for query_result in all_search_results) print(f"Total search results collected: {total_results}") print(f"High-confidence potential reports identified: {len(potential_reports)}") if potential_reports: print(f"\nüéØ TOP POTENTIAL 2023 IPCC 85-PAGE REPORTS:") # Sort by score (highest first) potential_reports.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True) for i, report in enumerate(potential_reports[:5], 1): # Show top 5 print(f"\n{i}. {report['title']}") print(f" URL: {report['url']}") print(f" Score: {report['score']}") print(f" Query: {report['query']}") print(f" Indicators:") print(f" - Official IPCC: {report['indicators']['official_ipcc']}") print(f" - PDF Document: {report['indicators']['is_pdf']}") print(f" - Has 2023: {report['indicators']['has_2023']}") print(f" - Has 85 pages: {report['indicators']['has_85_pages']}") print(f" - IPCC terms: {report['indicators']['matching_ipcc_terms']}") print(f" Snippet: {report['snippet'][:150]}...") else: print("\n‚ùå No high-confidence matches found.") print("Will need to try alternative search strategies or examine lower-scoring results.") print(f"\nüìä SEARCH STATISTICS:") print(f"Queries executed: {len(search_queries)}") print(f"Total results found: {total_results}") print(f"Potential reports identified: {len(potential_reports)}") print(f"Results saved to: {results_file}") print(f"\nNext step: Download and verify the most promising report(s) for 85-page specification.")

import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime print("=== SEARCHING FOR 2023 IPCC REPORT WITH 85-PAGE SPECIFICATION ===") print("=" * 70) # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with targeted search for 2023 IPCC 85-page report...") print() # Define specific search queries to locate the 2023 IPCC report with 85 pages search_queries = [ 'IPCC 2023 report 85 pages filetype:pdf', 'IPCC 2023 "85 pages" summary policymakers filetype:pdf', 'IPCC 2023 synthesis report 85 pages filetype:pdf', 'site:ipcc.ch 2023 report "85 pages" filetype:pdf', 'IPCC AR6 2023 synthesis report 85 pages', '"IPCC 2023" "85-page" OR "85 page" report filetype:pdf', 'IPCC sixth assessment 2023 synthesis 85 pages', 'IPCC AR6 synthesis report 2023 policymakers 85' ] print(f"Executing {len(search_queries)} targeted searches for 2023 IPCC 85-page report...\n") # Store all search results all_search_results = [] potential_reports = [] for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"Search {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 50) # Prepare API request parameters params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 15, "type": "search" } try: # Make API request to SerpAPI response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Store results with query context query_results = { 'query': query, 'results': results['organic_results'], 'search_number': i, 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() } all_search_results.append(query_results) # Analyze results for IPCC reports for j, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No URL') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') # Check for IPCC-specific indicators title_lower = title.lower() snippet_lower = snippet.lower() combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}" # Key indicators for IPCC 2023 reports ipcc_indicators = [ 'ipcc', '2023', 'synthesis', 'summary', 'policymakers', 'assessment', 'climate change', 'ar6' ] # Page count indicators page_indicators = ['85', 'page', 'pages'] matching_ipcc = [ind for ind in ipcc_indicators if ind in combined_text] matching_pages = [ind for ind in page_indicators if ind in combined_text] print(f"\n Result {j}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:200]}{'...' if len(snippet) > 200 else ''}") if matching_ipcc: print(f" ‚úì IPCC INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_ipcc)}") if matching_pages: print(f" üìÑ PAGE INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_pages)}") # High priority for official IPCC sites and PDF files is_official_ipcc = 'ipcc.ch' in link.lower() is_pdf = link.lower().endswith('.pdf') or 'filetype:pdf' in query has_2023 = '2023' in combined_text has_85_pages = '85' in combined_text and ('page' in combined_text) if is_official_ipcc: print(f" üèõÔ∏è OFFICIAL IPCC SOURCE") if is_pdf: print(f" üìã PDF DOCUMENT") if has_85_pages: print(f" üéØ 85-PAGE SPECIFICATION MENTIONED") # Score potential matches score = 0 if is_official_ipcc: score += 5 if is_pdf: score += 3 if has_2023: score += 3 if has_85_pages: score += 4 if 'synthesis' in combined_text: score += 2 if 'summary' in combined_text: score += 2 if 'policymakers' in combined_text: score += 2 if score >= 8: # High-confidence matches potential_reports.append({ 'title': title, 'url': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'query': query, 'score': score, 'indicators': { 'official_ipcc': is_official_ipcc, 'is_pdf': is_pdf, 'has_2023': has_2023, 'has_85_pages': has_85_pages, 'matching_ipcc_terms': matching_ipcc, 'matching_page_terms': matching_pages } }) print(f" ‚≠ê HIGH-CONFIDENCE MATCH (Score: {score})") else: print("No organic results found for this query") all_search_results.append({ 'query': query, 'results': [], 'search_number': i, 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() }) else: print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error during search {i}: {str(e)}") continue print("\n") print("\n" + "=" * 70) print("SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY") print("=" * 70) # import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime # First, let's check what search results we already have in workspace print("=== CHECKING EXISTING SEARCH RESULTS ===\n") # List workspace contents to see what files we have workspace_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.json')] print(f"Found {len(workspace_files)} JSON files in workspace:") for file in workspace_files: print(f" - {file}") # Find the most recent IPCC search results file ipcc_results_files = [f for f in workspace_files if 'ipcc_2023_85page_search_results' in f] if ipcc_results_files: # Use the most recent file (they have timestamps) latest_results_file = sorted(ipcc_results_files)[-1] results_path = f'workspace/{latest_results_file}' print(f"\nUsing latest search results file: {latest_results_file}") # First inspect the file structure before accessing it print("\n=== INSPECTING SEARCH RESULTS FILE STRUCTURE ===\n") with open(results_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print("Top-level keys in search results:") for key, value in search_data.items(): if isinstance(value, list): print(f" {key}: List with {len(value)} items") elif isinstance(value, dict): print(f" {key}: Dictionary with {len(value)} keys") else: print(f" {key}: {type(value).__name__} - {str(value)[:100]}...") # Examine potential_reports in detail if 'potential_reports' in search_data: potential_reports = search_data['potential_reports'] print(f"\n=== ANALYZING {len(potential_reports)} POTENTIAL REPORTS ===\n") # Sort by score (highest first) sorted_reports = sorted(potential_reports, key=lambda x: x.get('score', 0), reverse=True) print("Top candidates for 85-page IPCC 2023 report:") target_urls = [] for i, report in enumerate(sorted_reports[:5], 1): print(f"\n{i}. Score: {report.get('score', 0)}") print(f" Title: {report.get('title', 'No title')}") print(f" URL: {report.get('url', 'No URL')}") print(f" Query: {report.get('query', 'No query')}") # Check indicators indicators = report.get('indicators', {}) print(f" Indicators:") print(f" - Official IPCC: {indicators.get('official_ipcc', False)}") print(f" - PDF Document: {indicators.get('is_pdf', False)}") print(f" - Has 2023: {indicators.get('has_2023', False)}") print(f" - Has 85 pages: {indicators.get('has_85_pages', False)}") # Prioritize official IPCC PDFs with high scores if (indicators.get('official_ipcc', False) and indicators.get('is_pdf', False) and report.get('score', 0) >= 10): target_urls.append({ 'url': report.get('url'), 'title': report.get('title'), 'score': report.get('score', 0), 'filename': report.get('url', '').split('/')[-1] if report.get('url') else 'unknown.pdf' }) print(f"\n=== IDENTIFIED {len(target_urls)} HIGH-PRIORITY DOWNLOAD TARGETS ===\n") for i, target in enumerate(target_urls, 1): print(f"{i}. {target['title']} (Score: {target['score']})") print(f" URL: {target['url']}") print(f" Filename: {target['filename']}") # Download the top candidates to verify 85-page specification if target_urls: print(f"\n=== DOWNLOADING TOP CANDIDATES FOR VERIFICATION ===\n") downloaded_files = [] for i, target in enumerate(target_urls[:3], 1): # Download top 3 candidates print(f"Downloading {i}/{min(3, len(target_urls))}: {target['filename']}") print(f"URL: {target['url']}") try: # Set headers to mimic browser request headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'application/pdf,application/octet-stream,*/*', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9', 'Referer': 'https://www.ipcc.ch/' } response = requests.get(target['url'], headers=headers, timeout=60, stream=True) if response.status_code == 200: # Generate safe filename safe_filename = target['filename'] if not safe_filename.endswith('.pdf'): safe_filename += '.pdf' filepath = f"workspace/{safe_filename}" # Write file in chunks to handle large PDFs with open(filepath, 'wb') as f: for chunk in response.iter_content(chunk_size=8192): if chunk: f.write(chunk) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f"‚úÖ Successfully downloaded: {safe_filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)") downloaded_files.append({ 'filename': safe_filename, 'filepath': filepath, 'title': target['title'], 'url': target['url'], 'size_bytes': file_size, 'score': target['score'] }) else: print(f"‚ùå Download failed: HTTP {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"‚ùå Download error: {str(e)}") print() # Save download results if downloaded_files: download_results = { 'download_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'total_downloaded': len(downloaded_files), 'downloaded_files': downloaded_files, 'purpose': 'Verify 2023 IPCC report with 85-page specification', 'next_step': 'Parse PDFs to determine page count and identify the correct 85-page report' } download_log = f"workspace/ipcc_2023_downloads_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json" with open(download_log, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(download_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"=== DOWNLOAD SUMMARY ===\n") print(f"Successfully downloaded: {len(downloaded_files)} files") print(f"Download log saved to: {download_log}") print(f"\nDownloaded files:") for file_info in downloaded_files: print(f" - {file_info['filename']} ({file_info['size_bytes']:,} bytes)") print(f" Title: {file_info['title']}") print(f" Score: {file_info['score']}") print(f"\nüéØ NEXT STEP: Parse the downloaded PDFs to:") print(f" 1. Determine exact page count for each document") print(f" 2. Identify which document has exactly 85 pages") print(f" 3. Verify it's the correct 2023 IPCC report for nuclear energy analysis") else: print("‚ùå No files were successfully downloaded") print("Will need to try alternative download strategies") else: print("‚ùå No high-priority download targets identified") print("The search results may need refinement or alternative approaches") else: print("‚ùå No 'potential_reports' found in search results") print("Search results structure may be different than expected") else: print("‚ùå No previous IPCC search results found in workspace") print("Need to run the search phase first") print(f"\n=== CURRENT WORKSPACE STATUS ===\n") all_files = os.listdir('workspace') print(f"Total files in workspace: {len(all_files)}") for file in sorted(all_files): filepath = f'workspace/{file}' if os.path.isfile(filepath): size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f" - {file} ({size:,} bytes)")

import os import PyPDF2 import json from datetime import datetime print("=== PARSING DOWNLOADED IPCC PDFs TO VERIFY 85-PAGE SPECIFICATION ===") print("=" * 75) # First, let's inspect what PDF files we have in workspace workspace_files = os.listdir('workspace') pdf_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.endswith('.pdf')] print(f"Found {len(pdf_files)} PDF files in workspace:") for pdf_file in pdf_files: filepath = f'workspace/{pdf_file}' file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f" - {pdf_file} ({file_size:,} bytes)") if not pdf_files: print("‚ùå No PDF files found in workspace") print("Need to download the IPCC documents first") else: print(f"\n=== ANALYZING PAGE COUNTS FOR {len(pdf_files)} PDF DOCUMENTS ===\n") pdf_analysis = [] for pdf_file in pdf_files: filepath = f'workspace/{pdf_file}' print(f"Analyzing: {pdf_file}") print("-" * 50) try: # Open and read PDF file with open(filepath, 'rb') as file: pdf_reader = PyPDF2.PdfReader(file) # Get basic PDF information num_pages = len(pdf_reader.pages) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f"üìÑ Total pages: {num_pages}") print(f"üì¶ File size: {file_size:,} bytes") # Try to extract metadata metadata = pdf_reader.metadata if metadata: print(f"üìã Metadata:") if metadata.title: print(f" Title: {metadata.title}") if metadata.author: print(f" Author: {metadata.author}") if metadata.subject: print(f" Subject: {metadata.subject}") if metadata.creator: print(f" Creator: {metadata.creator}") if metadata.creation_date: print(f" Creation Date: {metadata.creation_date}") # Extract first few pages of text to identify document type print(f"\nüìñ Document Content Preview:") preview_text = "" pages_to_preview = min(3, num_pages) for page_num in range(pages_to_preview): try: page = pdf_reader.pages[page_num] page_text = page.extract_text() preview_text += f"\n--- Page {page_num + 1} ---\n" preview_text += page_text[:500] + "...\n" if len(page_text) > 500 else page_text + "\n" except Exception as e: preview_text += f"\n--- Page {page_num + 1} (extraction error) ---\n" preview_text += f"Error: {str(e)}\n" # Display preview (limited length) print(preview_text[:1500] + "..." if len(preview_text) > 1500 else preview_text) # Check if this is exactly 85 pages is_85_pages = (num_pages == 85) print(f"\nüéØ Is exactly 85 pages? {'‚úÖ YES' if is_85_pages else '‚ùå NO'}") # Analyze document type based on filename and content document_type = "Unknown" if "SYR_FullVolume" in pdf_file: document_type = "AR6 Synthesis Report - Full Volume" elif "SYR_LongerReport" in pdf_file: document_type = "AR6 Synthesis Report - Longer Report" elif "SYR_SPM" in pdf_file: document_type = "AR6 Synthesis Report - Summary for Policymakers" elif "WGI_TS" in pdf_file: document_type = "Working Group I - Technical Summary" elif "WGI_Chapter" in pdf_file: document_type = "Working Group I - Chapter" print(f"üìö Document Type: {document_type}") # Store analysis results pdf_analysis.append({ 'filename': pdf_file, 'filepath': filepath, 'num_pages': num_pages, 'file_size_bytes': file_size, 'is_85_pages': is_85_pages, 'document_type': document_type, 'metadata': { 'title': str(metadata.title) if metadata and metadata.title else None, 'author': str(metadata.author) if metadata and metadata.author else None, 'subject': str(metadata.subject) if metadata and metadata.subject else None, 'creator': str(metadata.creator) if metadata and metadata.creator else None, 'creation_date': str(metadata.creation_date) if metadata and metadata.creation_date else None }, 'preview_text': preview_text[:2000] # Store limited preview }) except Exception as e: print(f"‚ùå Error analyzing {pdf_file}: {str(e)}") pdf_analysis.append({ 'filename': pdf_file, 'filepath': filepath, 'num_pages': 0, 'file_size_bytes': os.path.getsize(filepath), 'is_85_pages': False, 'document_type': 'Error - Could not analyze', 'error': str(e) }) print("\n") # Save analysis results analysis_results = { 'analysis_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'total_pdfs_analyzed': len(pdf_files), 'pdf_analysis': pdf_analysis, 'search_objective': 'Find 2023 IPCC report with exactly 85 pages for nuclear energy analysis' } analysis_file = f"workspace/ipcc_pdf_page_analysis_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json" with open(analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print("=" * 75) print("PDF ANALYSIS SUMMARY") print("=" * 75) # Find documents with exactly 85 pages exact_85_page_docs = [doc for doc in pdf_analysis if doc.get('is_85_pages', False)] print(f"\nüìä ANALYSIS RESULTS:") print(f"Total PDFs analyzed: {len(pdf_analysis)}") print(f"Documents with exactly 85 pages: {len(exact_85_page_docs)}") print(f"\nüìÑ PAGE COUNT BREAKDOWN:") for doc in pdf_analysis: status = "üéØ TARGET (85 pages)" if doc.get('is_85_pages', False) else "üìñ Not target" print(f" - {doc['filename']}: {doc['num_pages']} pages {status}") print(f" Type: {doc.get('document_type', 'Unknown')}") if exact_85_page_docs: print(f"\n‚úÖ FOUND {len(exact_85_page_docs)} DOCUMENT(S) WITH EXACTLY 85 PAGES:") for i, doc in enumerate(exact_85_page_docs, 1): print(f"\n{i}. {doc['filename']}") print(f" üìÑ Pages: {doc['num_pages']}") print(f" üì¶ Size: {doc['file_size_bytes']:,} bytes") print(f" üìö Type: {doc.get('document_type', 'Unknown')}") print(f" üìã Title: {doc.get('metadata', {}).get('title', 'Not available')}") print(f" üìÖ Creation: {doc.get('metadata', {}).get('creation_date', 'Not available')}") # Check if this looks like the right document for nuclear energy analysis preview = doc.get('preview_text', '').lower() nuclear_indicators = ['nuclear', 'energy', 'power', 'electricity', 'renewable'] found_indicators = [ind for ind in nuclear_indicators if ind in preview] if found_indicators: print(f" üî¨ Nuclear/Energy indicators found: {', '.join(found_indicators)}") else: print(f" ‚ö†Ô∏è No obvious nuclear/energy indicators in preview") print(f"\nüéØ PLAN STATUS: SUCCESS") print(f"‚úÖ Located 2023 IPCC report with exactly 85 pages") print(f"‚úÖ Document ready for nuclear energy mention analysis") else: print(f"\n‚ùå NO DOCUMENTS WITH EXACTLY 85 PAGES FOUND") print(f"\nAvailable documents:") for doc in pdf_analysis: print(f" - {doc['filename']}: {doc['num_pages']} pages") print(f"\nüîç RECOMMENDATION:") print(f"The 85-page specification might refer to:") print(f"1. A specific section or chapter within a larger document") print(f"2. A different version/format of the IPCC report") print(f"3. A summary or condensed version not yet downloaded") # Check if any document is close to 85 pages close_matches = [doc for doc in pdf_analysis if abs(doc['num_pages'] - 85) <= 10] if close_matches: print(f"\nüìä CLOSE MATCHES (within 10 pages of 85):") for doc in close_matches: print(f" - {doc['filename']}: {doc['num_pages']} pages (diff: {abs(doc['num_pages'] - 85)})") print(f"\nDetailed analysis saved to: {analysis_file}") print(f"\n=== ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===")

Python Code python
import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime print("=== TARGETED SEARCH FOR IPCC AR6 SYNTHESIS REPORT LONGER REPORT (85 PAGES) ===") print("=" * 80) # Based on search results analysis, let's try to download the "Longer Report" version # which was specifically mentioned in search results as having 85 pages # Check if we already have search results to reference workspace_files = os.listdir('workspace') search_files = [f for f in workspace_files if 'search_results' in f and f.endswith('.json')] if search_files: latest_search_file = sorted(search_files)[-1] print(f"Referencing previous search results: {latest_search_file}\n") else: print("No previous search results found\n") # Direct URLs to try based on IPCC structure and search results target_urls = [ { 'url': 'https://www.ipcc.ch/report/ar6/syr/downloads/report/IPCC_AR6_SYR_LongerReport.pdf', 'filename': 'IPCC_AR6_SYR_LongerReport.pdf', 'description': 'AR6 Synthesis Report - Longer Report (most likely 85-page candidate)', 'priority': 1 }, { 'url': 'https://www.ipcc.ch/report/ar6/syr/downloads/report/IPCC_AR6_SYR_SPM.pdf', 'filename': 'IPCC_AR6_SYR_SPM.pdf', 'description': 'AR6 Synthesis Report - Summary for Policymakers', 'priority': 2 } ] print(f"Attempting to download {len(target_urls)} additional IPCC documents:\n") downloaded_files = [] for i, target in enumerate(target_urls, 1): print(f"Download {i}/{len(target_urls)}: {target['filename']}") print(f"URL: {target['url']}") print(f"Description: {target['description']}") # Check if file already exists filepath = f"workspace/{target['filename']}" if os.path.exists(filepath): print(f"‚úÖ File already exists: {target['filename']}") file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) downloaded_files.append({ 'filename': target['filename'], 'filepath': filepath, 'url': target['url'], 'size_bytes': file_size, 'status': 'already_exists', 'description': target['description'] }) else: try: # Set headers to mimic browser request headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'application/pdf,application/octet-stream,*/*', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9', 'Referer': 'https://www.ipcc.ch/' } response = requests.get(target['url'], headers=headers, timeout=60, stream=True) if response.status_code == 200: # Write file in chunks with open(filepath, 'wb') as f: for chunk in response.iter_content(chunk_size=8192): if chunk: f.write(chunk) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f"‚úÖ Successfully downloaded: {target['filename']} ({file_size:,} bytes)") downloaded_files.append({ 'filename': target['filename'], 'filepath': filepath, 'url': target['url'], 'size_bytes': file_size, 'status': 'newly_downloaded', 'description': target['description'] }) else: print(f"‚ùå Download failed: HTTP {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"‚ùå Download error: {str(e)}") print() # Now let's analyze the page counts of all PDF files in workspace print("=== ANALYZING ALL PDF FILES FOR 85-PAGE SPECIFICATION ===") print("=" * 60) all_pdf_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.pdf')] print(f"Found {len(all_pdf_files)} PDF files in workspace:\n") pdf_analysis = [] # Import PyPDF2 for PDF analysis try: import PyPDF2 for pdf_file in all_pdf_files: filepath = f'workspace/{pdf_file}' print(f"Analyzing: {pdf_file}") print("-" * 40) try: with open(filepath, 'rb') as file: pdf_reader = PyPDF2.PdfReader(file) num_pages = len(pdf_reader.pages) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f"üìÑ Pages: {num_pages}") print(f"üì¶ Size: {file_size:,} bytes") # Check for 85 pages is_85_pages = (num_pages == 85) if is_85_pages: print(f"üéØ *** THIS IS THE 85-PAGE DOCUMENT WE'RE LOOKING FOR! ***") else: print(f"üìñ Not the target (need exactly 85 pages)") # Summary print("=" * 60) print("FINAL ANALYSIS SUMMARY") print("=" * 60) if pdf_analysis: # Find 85-page documents target_docs = [doc for doc in pdf_analysis if doc.get('is_85_pages', False)] print(f"\nüìä RESULTS:") print(f"Total PDF files analyzed: {len(pdf_analysis)}") print(f"Documents with exactly 85 pages: {len(target_docs)}") print(f"\nüìÑ ALL DOCUMENTS:") for doc in pdf_analysis: status = "üéØ TARGET (85 pages)" if doc.get('is_85_pages', False) else "üìñ Not target" print(f" - {doc['filename']}: {doc['num_pages']} pages {status}") print(f" Type: {doc.get('document_type', 'Unknown')}") if target_docs: print(f"\n‚úÖ SUCCESS: FOUND THE 85-PAGE IPCC 2023 REPORT!") for doc in target_docs: print(f"\nüéØ TARGET DOCUMENT IDENTIFIED:") print(f" üìÅ Filename: {doc['filename']}") print(f" üìÑ Pages: {doc['num_pages']} (exactly 85 as specified)") print(f" üì¶ Size: {doc['file_size_bytes']:,} bytes") print(f" üìö Type: {doc.get('document_type', 'Unknown')}") print(f" üìç Location: workspace/{doc['filename']}") print(f"\nüéØ PLAN STATUS: COMPLETE ‚úÖ") print(f"‚úÖ Successfully located 2023 IPCC report with exactly 85 pages") print(f"‚úÖ Document is ready for nuclear energy mention analysis") print(f"\nüìã Next step: Parse the 85-page document to analyze nuclear energy mentions") else: print(f"\n‚ùå NO 85-PAGE DOCUMENT FOUND") print(f"\nüîç Available documents and their page counts:") for doc in pdf_analysis: print(f" - {doc['filename']}: {doc['num_pages']} pages") print(f"\nüí° RECOMMENDATIONS:") print(f"1. import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime print("=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR ALTERNATIVE 2023 IPCC 85-PAGE DOCUMENTS ===") print("=" * 75) # Based on the analysis, we haven't found an exact 85-page document yet. # Let's try a more comprehensive search for alternative IPCC 2023 documents # that might match the 85-page specification. # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with alternative search strategies...\n") # Define more specific search queries focusing on exact 85-page specification alternative_queries = [ 'IPCC 2023 "85 pages" "synthesis report" -site:climatecasechart.com filetype:pdf', 'site:ipcc.ch "85 pages" 2023 synthesis report filetype:pdf', 'IPCC AR6 2023 "eighty-five pages" OR "85-page" filetype:pdf', 'IPCC 2023 synthesis "85 pp" OR "85p" filetype:pdf', 'IPCC "Climate Change 2023" "85 pages" summary filetype:pdf', '"IPCC AR6 Synthesis Report" 2023 "85 pages" -climatecasechart filetype:pdf', 'IPCC 2023 synthesis report "page 85" "total pages" filetype:pdf', 'site:unfccc.int OR site:un.org IPCC 2023 "85 pages" synthesis filetype:pdf' ] print(f"Executing {len(alternative_queries)} alternative search queries...\n") # Store all search results alternative_results = [] potential_85_page_docs = [] for i, query in enumerate(alternative_queries, 1): print(f"Alternative Search {i}/{len(alternative_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 60) # Prepare API request parameters params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 20, # Increased for better coverage "type": "search" } try: # Make API request to SerpAPI response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Store results with query context query_results = { 'query': query, 'results': results['organic_results'], 'search_number': i, 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() } alternative_results.append(query_results) # Analyze results for new potential documents for j, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No URL') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') # Check for new indicators title_lower = title.lower() snippet_lower = snippet.lower() combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}" # Key indicators for 85-page documents page_indicators = ['85 pages', '85-page', '85 pp', 'eighty-five pages', 'page 85'] ipcc_2023_indicators = ['ipcc', '2023', 'synthesis', 'climate change'] matching_pages = [ind for ind in page_indicators if ind in combined_text] matching_ipcc = [ind for ind in ipcc_2023_indicators if ind in combined_text] if j <= 5: # Show top 5 results for each query print(f"\n Result {j}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:150]}{'...' if len(snippet) > 150 else ''}") if matching_pages: print(f" üìÑ PAGE INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_pages)}") if matching_ipcc: print(f" üèõÔ∏è IPCC INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_ipcc)}") # Score potential matches differently than before is_pdf = link.lower().endswith('.pdf') or 'filetype:pdf' in query has_85_pages = any(ind in combined_text for ind in page_indicators) has_ipcc_2023 = 'ipcc' in combined_text and '2023' in combined_text is_official = any(domain in link.lower() for domain in ['ipcc.ch', 'unfccc.int', 'un.org']) # New documents we haven't seen before new_document = link not in [doc.get('url', '') for doc in potential_85_page_docs] if has_85_pages and has_ipcc_2023 and is_pdf and new_document: score = 0 if is_official: score += 5 if is_pdf: score += 3 if has_85_pages: score += 4 if 'synthesis' in combined_text: score += 2 if '2023' in combined_text: score += 3 potential_85_page_docs.append({ 'title': title, 'url': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'query': query, 'score': score, 'indicators': { 'is_official': is_official, 'is_pdf': is_pdf, 'has_85_pages': has_85_pages, 'has_ipcc_2023': has_ipcc_2023, 'matching_page_terms': matching_pages, 'matching_ipcc_terms': matching_ipcc } }) if j <= 5: # Only show for top results print(f" ‚≠ê POTENTIAL 85-PAGE DOCUMENT (Score: {score})") else: print("No organic results found for this query") alternative_results.append({ 'query': query, 'results': [], 'search_number': i, 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() }) else: print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error during alternative search {i}: {str(e)}") continue print("\n") print("\n" + "=" * 75) print("ALTERNATIVE SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY") print("=" * 75) # Save all alternative search results timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") alt_results_file = f"workspace/ipcc_85page_alternative_search_{timestamp}.json" with open(alt_results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump({ 'search_timestamp': timestamp, 'search_strategy': 'Alternative search for IPCC 2023 85-page documents', 'total_queries': len(alternative_queries), 'queries_executed': alternative_queries, 'alternative_search_results': alternative_results, 'potential_85_page_documents': potential_85_page_docs }, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"Alternative search results saved to: {alt_results_file}") # Analyze findings total_results = sum(len(query_result['results']) for query_result in alternative_results) print(f"Total alternative search results collected: {total_results}") print(f"New potential 85-page documents identified: {len(potential_85_page_docs)}") if potential_85_page_docs: print(f"\nüîç NEW POTENTIAL 85-PAGE DOCUMENTS FOUND:") # Sort by score (highest first) potential_85_page_docs.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True) for i, doc in enumerate(potential_85_page_docs[:5], 1): # Show top 5 print(f"\n{i}. {doc['title']}") print(f" URL: {doc['url']}") print(f" Score: {doc['score']}") print(f" Query: {doc['query']}") print(f" Indicators:") print(f" - Official Source: {doc['indicators']['is_official']}") print(f" - PDF Document: {doc['indicators']['is_pdf']}") print(f" - Has 85 pages: {doc['indicators']['has_85_pages']}") print(f" - IPCC 2023: {doc['indicators']['has_ipcc_2023']}") print(f" - Page terms: {doc['indicators']['matching_page_terms']}") print(f" Snippet: {doc['snippet'][:150]}...") # Try to download the most promising new documents print(f"\n=== DOWNLOADING TOP NEW CANDIDATES ===\n") new_downloads = [] for doc in potential_85_page_docs[:3]: # Try top 3 new candidates filename = doc['url'].split('/')[-1] if not filename.endswith('.pdf'): filename += '.pdf' filepath = f"workspace/{filename}" # Check if we already have this file if os.path.exists(filepath): print(f"‚úÖ Already have: {filename}") continue print(f"Downloading: {filename}") print(f"URL: {doc['url']}") try: headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'application/pdf,application/octet-stream,*/*', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9' } response = requests.get(doc['url'], headers=headers, timeout=60, stream=True) if response.status_code == 200: with open(filepath, 'wb') as f: for chunk in response.iter_content(chunk_size=8192): if chunk: f.write(chunk) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f"‚úÖ Downloaded: {filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)") new_downloads.append(filename) else: print(f"‚ùå Download failed: HTTP {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"‚ùå Download error: {str(e)}") print() if new_downloads: print(f"\nüì• NEW DOWNLOADS COMPLETED: {len(new_downloads)} files") for filename in new_downloads: print(f" - {filename}") print(f"\nüîç Next step: Analyze these new documents for exact page count") else: print(f"\nüìã No new documents downloaded (may already exist or download failed)") else: print(f"\n‚ùå NO NEW POTENTIAL 85-PAGE DOCUMENTS FOUND") print(f"The alternative search strategies did not identify additional candidates.") # Final status assessment print(f"\n=== CURRENT STATUS ASSESSMENT ===\n") # Check what we have in workspace now current_pdfs = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.pdf')] print(f"Total PDF documents in workspace: {len(current_pdfs)}") print(f"\nüìã PLAN STATUS EVALUATION:") print(f"‚úÖ Successfully searched for 2023 IPCC reports") print(f"‚úÖ Downloaded multiple official IPCC 2023 documents") print(f"‚úÖ Analyzed page counts of all available documents") print(f"‚ùå No document found with exactly 85 pages") print(f"\nüí° RECOMMENDATION:") print(f"Given that we have thoroughly searched and analyzed official IPCC 2023 documents,") print(f"and the closest match is the 81-page 'Longer Report', we should consider:") print(f"1. The 85-page specification may be incorrect or refer to a different document") print(f"2. Proceed with the 81-page AR6 Synthesis Report Longer Report as the closest match") print(f"3. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with alternative search strategies...\n") # Define more specific search queries focusing on exact 85-page specification alternative_queries = [ 'IPCC 2023 "85 pages" "synthesis report" -site:climatecasechart.com filetype:pdf', 'site:ipcc.ch "85 pages" 2023 synthesis report filetype:pdf', 'IPCC AR6 2023 "eighty-five pages" OR "85-page" filetype:pdf', 'IPCC 2023 synthesis "85 pp" OR "85p" filetype:pdf', 'IPCC "Climate Change 2023" "85 pages" summary filetype:pdf', '"IPCC AR6 Synthesis Report" 2023 "85 pages" -climatecasechart filetype:pdf', 'IPCC 2023 synthesis report "page 85" "total pages" filetype:pdf', 'site:unfccc.int OR site:un.org IPCC 2023 "85 pages" synthesis filetype:pdf' ] print(f"Executing {len(alternative_queries)} alternative search queries...\n") # Store all search results alternative_results = [] potential_85_page_docs = [] for i, query in enumerate(alternative_queries, 1): print(f"Alternative Search {i}/{len(alternative_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 60) # Prepare API request parameters params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 20, # Increased for better coverage "type": "search" } try: # Make API request to SerpAPI response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Store results with query context query_results = { 'query': query, 'results': results['organic_results'], 'search_number': i, 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() } alternative_results.append(query_results) # Analyze results for new potential documents for j, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No URL') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') # Check for new indicators title_lower = title.lower() snippet_lower = snippet.lower() combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}" # Key indicators for 85-page documents page_indicators = ['85 pages', '85-page', '85 pp', 'eighty-five pages', 'page 85'] ipcc_2023_indicators = ['ipcc', '2023', 'synthesis', 'climate change'] matching_pages = [ind for ind in page_indicators if ind in combined_text] matching_ipcc = [ind for ind in ipcc_2023_indicators if ind in combined_text] if j <= 5: # Show top 5 results for each query print(f"\n Result {j}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:150]}{'...' if len(snippet) > 150 else ''}") if matching_pages: print(f" üìÑ PAGE INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_pages)}") if matching_ipcc: print(f" üèõÔ∏è IPCC INDICATORS: {', '.join(matching_ipcc)}") # Score potential matches differently than before is_pdf = link.lower().endswith('.pdf') or 'filetype:pdf' in query has_85_pages = any(ind in combined_text for ind in page_indicators) has_ipcc_2023 = 'ipcc' in combined_text and '2023' in combined_text is_official = any(domain in link.lower() for domain in ['ipcc.ch', 'unfccc.int', 'un.org']) # New documents we haven't seen before new_document = link not in [doc.get('url', '') for doc in potential_85_page_docs] if has_85_pages and has_ipcc_2023 and is_pdf and new_document: score = 0 if is_official: score += 5 if is_pdf: score += 3 if has_85_pages: score += 4 if 'synthesis' in combined_text: score += 2 if '2023' in combined_text: score += 3 potential_85_page_docs.append({ 'title': title, 'url': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'query': query, 'score': score, 'indicators': { 'is_official': is_official, 'is_pdf': is_pdf, 'has_85_pages': has_85_pages, 'has_ipcc_2023': has_ipcc_2023, 'matching_page_terms': matching_pages, 'matching_ipcc_terms': matching_ipcc } }) if j <= 5: # Only show for top results print(f" ‚≠ê POTENTIAL 85-PAGE DOCUMENT (Score: {score})") else: print("No organic results found for this query") alternative_results.append({ 'query': query, 'results': [], 'search_number': i, 'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat() }) else: print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error during alternative search {i}: {str(e)}") continue print("\n") print("\n" + "=" * 75) print("ALTERNATIVE SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY") print("=" * 75) #
